 //keep modal window of jQuery not scrollable
 $(document).scroll(function (e) {
 
     if ($(".ui-widget-overlay")) //the dialog has popped up in modal view
     {
         //fix the overlay so it scrolls down with the page
         $(".ui-widget-overlay").css({
             position: 'fixed',
             top: '0'
         });
 
 
         if ($(".ui-dialog").size() > 0) {
             //get the current popup position of the dialog box
             pos = $(".ui-dialog").position();
 
             //adjust the dialog box so that it scrolls as you scroll the page
             $(".ui-dialog").css({
                 position: 'fixed',
                 top: pos.y
             });
         }
     }
 });

 function ffTimer() {
         if (document.forms['search_1'].query.value.trim() != '') return true;
         Timer();
         return false;
     }
 
     var str = 'white';
     var ii = 0;
     var timerID = null;
     var timerRunning = false;
 
     function Timer() {
         if (ii % 2 == 1 )
             str = 'white';
         else
             str = 'red';
         ii++;
         document.forms['search_1'].query.style.backgroundColor = str;
         timerID =  setTimeout("Timer()", 100 );
         timerRunning = true;
         if (ii==6) {
             if(timerRunning) clearTimeout(timerID);
             timerRunning=false;
             ii=0;
         }
 
     }

     function isKeyboardEvent(event) {

 var currentCartPopUp = null;
     var currentCartPopUpHasMouse = false;
     function showCartPopup(popup){
         if (currentCartPopUpHasMouse) {
             return
         }
         if (currentCartPopUp && currentCartPopUp!=popup) {
             currentCartPopUp.hide();
         }
         currentCartPopUp = popup;
         if (currentCartPopUp) {
             currentCartPopUp.show();
         }
     }
     $('#cart_state_info_id').mouseover(function(){
         currentCartPopUpHasMouse=false;
         showCartPopup( $('#pearl-dropdown-basket_view'));
     }).mouseleave(function(){
         currentCartPopUpHasMouse=false;
         showCartPopup(null);
     });
     $('#pearl-dropdown-basket_view')
         .mouseenter(function(){
             currentCartPopUpHasMouse=true;
         }).mouseleave(function(){
         currentCartPopUpHasMouse=false;
         showCartPopup(null);
     });
     $(document).click(function(){showCartPopup(null)});
 var coClickedProducts = $('div[id^="ppopup"]');

 function setCookie(name, value, days) {
             if (days) {
                 var date = new Date();
                 date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                 var expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString()
             } else var expires = "";
             document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/"
         }
         function getCookie(name) {
             var nameEQ = name + "=";
             var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
             for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                 var c = ca[i];
                 while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
                 if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length)
             }
             return null
         }
         function delCookie(name) {
             setCookie(name, "", -1)
         }
 (function ($) {
 
             /**
              * @function
              * @property {object} jQuery plugin which runs handler function once specified element is inserted into the DOM
              * @param {function} handler A function to execute at the time when the element is inserted
              * @param {bool} shouldRunHandlerOnce Optional: if true, handler is unbound after its first invocation
              * @example $(selector).waitUntilExists(function);
              */
 
             $.fn.waitUntilExists = function (handler, shouldRunHandlerOnce, isChild) {
                 var found = 'found';
                 var $this = $(this.selector);
                 var $elements = $this.not(function () {
                     return $(this).data(found);
                 }).each(handler).data(found, true);
 
                 if (!isChild) {
                     (window.waitUntilExists_Intervals = window.waitUntilExists_Intervals || {})[this.selector] =
                             window.setInterval(function () {
                                 $this.waitUntilExists(handler, shouldRunHandlerOnce, true);
                             }, 500)
                     ;
                 }
                 else if (shouldRunHandlerOnce && $elements.length) {
                     window.clearInterval(window.waitUntilExists_Intervals[this.selector]);
                 }
                 return $this;
             }
         }(jQuery));
 
 
         $('#gts-checkbox').waitUntilExists(function () {
             $('#gts-checkbox').click(function (e) {
                 console.log("Clicked on YES button");
                 $.ajax({
                     type: "POST",
                     method: "POST",
                     url: "/google/gts/switchmarker.do",
                     data: "gts=true",
                     success: function (msg) {
                         console.log("GTS send: " + msg);
                     }
                 });
             });
         }, true);

                 $.ajax({

                     method: "POST",
                     url: "/google/gts/switchmarker.do",
                     data: "gts=false",
                     success: function (msg) {
                         console.log("GTS send: " + msg);
                     }
                 });
                 e.preventDefault();
             });
         }, true);

 $(document).ready(function() {
 
             $('.images_cat2xxx_578x400_png').attr('src', "/images/cat2xxx_578x357.png");

 var userInputTerm = null;
     var lastSelectedAutocompleteTerm = null;
     var lastSelectedSuggestion = null;
     var regExp = /[';:\-_!@"$%^?&\*\(\)\+=|\\/{}\[\]<>\.\~`?#]/g;
     $.fn.searchAutocompleteInitialize(
             "/search/autocomplete.do;jsessionid=g8A124796120A0DE2C8500E28A330CFF0",
             2000,
             3000,
             5,
             "#topSearchInput");
     $("#topSearchInput").on("autocompleteselect", function(event,ui) {
         //console.log("1 autocompleteselect '" + userInputTerm + "'");
         lastSelectedAutocompleteTerm = $("<div>" + ui.item.suggestion + "</div>").text();
         if (!isKeyboardEvent(event)) {
             $('#topSearchInput').val(lastSelectedAutocompleteTerm);
         }
 
         //console.log("2 autocompleteselect '" + userInputTerm + "'");
 
 
         $( "input[name='newff']" ).click();
         return false;
     });
     $("#topSearchInput").on("autocompletefocus", function(event,ui) {
         if ((typeof ui != 'undefined') && (typeof ui.item != 'undefined') && (typeof ui.item.suggestion != 'undefined')) {
             //console.log("autocompletefocus '" + ui.item.suggestion + "'");
             if (isKeyboardEvent(event)) {
                 $('#topSearchInput').val($("<div>" + ui.item.suggestion + "</div>").text());
                 lastSelectedSuggestion = $("<div>" + ui.item.suggestion + "</div>").text();
 
             }
         }
         return false;
     });
     $("#topSearchInput").on( "autocompleteopen", function( event, ui ) {
         //console.log("1 autocompleteopen '" + userInputTerm + "-" + $('#topSearchInput').val() + "'");
         if (userInputTerm === null) {
             userInputTerm = $('#topSearchInput').val();
         }
         //console.log("2 autocompleteopen '" + userInputTerm + "-" + $('#topSearchInput').val() + "'");
     } );
     $("#topSearchForm").submit(function(event) {
 
         //console.log("1" + lastSelectedAutocompleteTerm+"-"+lastSelectedSuggestion+"-"+$('#topSearchInput').val());
         if (userInputTerm && ($('#topSearchInput').val() || lastSelectedAutocompleteTerm)) {
             var usedQuery =  ($('#topSearchInput').val() != null)?$('#topSearchInput').val():lastSelectedAutocompleteTerm;
 
             
             //console.log("2 '" + userInputTerm + "-" + usedQuery+"'");
             var form = this;
             event.preventDefault();
             $.ajax({
               //  async: false,
                 method: "POST",
                 url: "/search/autocomplete_trace.do",
                 data: { searched_query: userInputTerm, proposed_query: lastSelectedAutocompleteTerm, used_query: usedQuery }
             }).done(function(data) {
                 //alert('done')
                 userInputTerm = null;
                 form.submit();
             });
             
             if (lastSelectedAutocompleteTerm) {
                 $("#topSearchForm").find("input[name='query_type']").val("4");
             }
         }
         if (lastSelectedSuggestion || $(lastSelectedSuggestion).length > 0) {
             if (lastSelectedSuggestion.trim().replace (regExp, ' ').replace(/ +/g, ' ')
                     === $('#topSearchInput').val().trim().replace (regExp, ' ').replace(/ +/g, ' ')) {
                 $("#topSearchForm").find("input[name='query_type']").val("4");
             }
         }
         return ffTimer();
     });

                     //clearInterval(pearlTopTabRowInterval);

         })
